questions to help your child prepare for each step towards the 11+ exams. \r\n\r\nWhat this means is that your child can answer questions on a subtopic and retake the same subtopic and be given a different set of questions.  Not the same questions in a different order but a different set of questions.  There is no limit to how many tests your child can take.\r\n\r\nThe Year 5 Maths PRO App covers 7 topics that include 39 subtopics which cover the Year 5 syllabus in the UK.\r\n\r\nEach subtopic has 10 questions which make up a test.  \r\nAt the end of the test the child is rewarded with an award.\r\nA diamond for 100% \r\nA gold star for 90 to 100%\r\nA silver star for 70 to 90%\r\nA bronze star for 50 to 70%\r\nA red star for less than 50%\r\n\r\nUp to 10 awards per subtopic can be displayed. This enables the parent to see easily how their child is performing. This also motivates the child to want to get higher awards and better marks.\r\n\r\nThere are 39 subtopics categorized as follows:\r\n\r\nNumbers\r\n\r\n1.\tWrite\r\n2.\tCounting in Powers of 10\r\n3.\tPlace Value\r\n4.\tRounding\r\n5.\tCompare\r\n6.\tPrime\r\n7.\tSquare and Cube\r\n8.\tRoman Numerals\r\n\r\nCalculations\r\n\r\n9.\tAddition\r\n10.\tSubtraction\r\n11.\tMultiplication\r\n12.\tDivision\r\n13.\tEstimating\r\n14.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nFractions\r\n\r\n15.\t Simplify\r\n16.\tAddition\r\n17.\tSubtraction\r\n18.\tMultiplication\r\n19.\tConvert\r\n20.\tSolve Problems\r\n\r\nDecimals\r\n\r\n21.\t Addition\r\n22.\t Subtraction\r\n23.\tDividing by 10 or 100\r\n24.\t Place Value\r\n25.\t Rounding\r\n26.\t Compare\r\n27.\tConvert\r\n28.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nMeasurements\r\n\r\n29.\t Length Mass and Volume\r\n30.\t Area and Perimeter \r\n31.\tEstimating Volume\r\n32.\t Time\r\n33.\t Money\r\n34.\t Solve Problems\r\n\r\nGeometry\r\n\r\n35.\t Angles\r\n36.\tNets\r\n37.\t Coordinates\r\n38.\t Reflection\r\n\r\nStatistics\r\n\r\n39.\tCharts\r\n\r\nTEST RESULTS\r\nOn the completion of each test the user is given a summary of questions answered correctly and incorrectly, the percentage achieved in the test and the time taken on each test.
